    function cspThrottleFunc(limit) {
        var reqCount = 0;
        return function (event) {
            var cspReportMapping = {
                'documentURI': 'document-uri', 'referrer': 'referrer',
                'violatedDirective': 'violated-directive', 'effectiveDirective': 'effective-directive',
                'originalPolicy': 'original-policy', 'disposition': 'disposition',
                'blockedURI': 'blocked-uri', 'lineNumber': 'line-number',
                'columnNumber': 'column-number', 'sourceFile': 'source-file',
                'statusCode': 'status-code', 'sample': 'script-sample'
            };
            if (reqCount <= limit) {
                cspjson = { 'csp-report': {} };
                for (var i = 0; i < Object.keys(cspReportMapping).length; i++) {
                    var tempKey = Object.keys(cspReportMapping)[i];

                        cspjson['csp-report'][cspReportMapping[tempKey]] = event[tempKey];
                    }
                }

                xhr.setRequestHeader('content-type', 'application/csp-report');
                xhr.send(JSON.stringify(cspjson));
                reqCount++
            }
        }
    }

<script data-deferred="mcm-init" data-mcm-hash-id="4" nonce="5W4WuESlszc="> 
    (function() {      

        var toFetchSequentially = [];
        var toFetchInParallel = [];           

        window.loadNextDeferredScript = function() {
            if (toFetchSequentially.length === 0) {
                ShellASPX.PreShellLoadedFunc();
                window.loadNextDeferredScript = function() {
                    // run just once
                };
            } else {
                var script = toFetchSequentially.shift();
                script.setAttribute('src', script.getAttribute('data-deferred-src'));
            }
        };

        window.handlePageReady = function() {     
            var deferredScripts = document.getElementsByTagName('script');

            for (var i=0; i<deferredScripts.length; i++) {
                var s = deferredScripts[i];
                if (s.getAttribute('data-deferred-src') && !s.noModule) {
                    toFetchSequentially.push(s);
                }
            }  

            var deferredStylesheets = document.getElementsByTagName('link');
            for (var i=0; i<deferredStylesheets.length; i++) {
                var s = deferredStylesheets[i];
                if (s.getAttribute('rel') === 'stylesheet' && s.getAttribute('data-deferred-href')) toFetchInParallel.push(s);
            }       


            loadNextDeferredScript();
    
            for (var i=0; i<toFetchInParallel.length; i++) {
                var s = toFetchInParallel[i];
                s.setAttribute('href', s.getAttribute('data-deferred-href'));
            }
                
            toFetchInParallel = [];
        };

    })();  
    </script>        <script data-mcm-hash-id="8">
        if (window.addEventListener) {
            window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', window.handlePageReady);            
        } else {
            // IE8
            window.attachEvent('onload', window.handlePageReady);
        }</script>

id="PrsnttnStrucBase_638689806927350230KOLR"><div class="aq PrsnttnHdrCntnr" id="PrsnttnHdrCntnr_638689806927350257JNDK"><h3 class="jq">Compression Springs </h3></div><div><div class="ap"><div class="am aw ImgsCntnr"><div class="horizImgs ImgGrid"><div><div class="am az GridCell" colspan="1" style="width:87px;padding-right:0px;padding-left:0px;padding-top:0px;"><div class="aj ImgCaptionCntnrHover" id="ImgCaptionCntnr_638689806926132156CPHZ" mcm-large-src="/mvC/Contents/gfx/ImageCache/943/9434K118p1-d03d-digitall@1x_636987803408256835.png?ver=ImageNotFound" mcm-large-srcset="/mvC/Contents/gfx/ImageCache/943/9434K118p1-d03d-digitall@1x_636987803408256835.png?ver=ImageNotFound,/mvC/Contents/gfx/ImageCache/943/9434K118p1-d03d-digitall@2x_636987803408256835.png?ver=ImageNotFound,/mvC/Contents/gfx/ImageCache/943/9434K118p1-d03d-digitall@3x_636987803408256835.png?ver=ImageNotFound,/mvC/Contents/gfx/ImageCache/943/9434K118p1-d03d-digitall@4x_636987803408256835.png?ver=ImageNotFound"><img alt=""></div></div><div class="clearDiv"></div></div></div></div><div class="am"><div class="CpyCntnr" style="width:700px;"><p class="ap PrsnttnCpy"><span class="Wrd">As you</span> squeeze a compression <span class="Wrd">spring,</span> it pushes back to return to its original <span class="Wrd">length.</span> Spring rate is the amount of force required for every inch of compression <span class="Wrd">or,</span> for metric <span class="Wrd">springs,</span> millimeter of <span class="Wrd">compression.</span> The higher the spring <span class="Wrd">rate,</span> the harder it is to compress the <span class="Wrd">spring.</span></p><p class="ap PrsnttnCpy"><span class="ad">Chrome</span><span class="ad">-</span><span class="ad">silicon</span> <span class="ad">steel</span> springs have a high tensile strength for reliable operation over a long <span class="Wrd">lifetime.</span></p><p class="ap PrsnttnCpy"><span class="ad">Zinc</span><span class="ad">-</span><span class="ad">plated</span> springs have mild corrosion <span class="Wrd">resistance.</span></p><p class="ap PrsnttnCpy">Springs <span class="ad">with</span> <span class="ad">closed</span> <span class="ad">and</span> <span class="ad">ground</span> <span class="ad">ends</span> sit <span class="Wrd">flat,</span> so they wont <span class="Wrd">buckle.</span></p><p class="PrsnttnCpy"><img class="jx" title="" src="https://images1.mcmaster.com/mvC/gfx/CADTriadIcon.svg?ver=1655309014" data-filterwithidind="False" width="33" height="20" alt="3D CAD models available">For technical drawings and 3-D models, click on a part number.</p></div></div><div class="clearDiv"></div></div><div class="SubPrsnttnCntnr" style="width:1035px;"><div class="SubPrsnttnGrid"><div class="ar"
